\hypertarget{complexheatmapux7ed3ux679cux5206ux6790ux548cux53efux89c6ux5316}{%
\section{ComplexHeatmap结果分析和可视化}\label{complexheatmapux7ed3ux679cux5206ux6790ux548cux53efux89c6ux5316}}

\url{https://github.com/cafferychen777/ggpicrust2}

ggpicrust2是一个综合软件包，旨在为分析和解释 PICRUSt2
功能预测结果提供无缝且直观的解决方案。它提供了广泛的功能，包括通路名称/描述注释、高级差异丰度
(differential abundance, DA) 方法以及 DA 结果的可视化。

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# 软件检测和安装}
\CommentTok{\# 安装并加载必要的包}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{requireNamespace}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"ComplexHeatmap"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)) \{}
\NormalTok{    BiocManager}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{install}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"ComplexHeatmap"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{requireNamespace}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"pheatmap"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{install.packages}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"pheatmap"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(ComplexHeatmap)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\end{verbatim}

\hypertarget{ux6570ux636eux5bfcux5165}{%
\subsection{数据导入}\label{ux6570ux636eux5bfcux5165}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# 设置随机种子以保证结果可重复}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{123}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# 创建一个更大规模的随机矩阵作为示例数据}
\NormalTok{data\_large }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{matrix}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rnorm}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1000}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{nrow =} \DecValTok{50}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{ncol =} \DecValTok{20}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(data\_large) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"基因"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{50}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(data\_large) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"样本"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{20}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{ux6570ux636eux5904ux7406}{%
\subsection{数据处理}\label{ux6570ux636eux5904ux7406}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# 对行（基因）进行K{-}means聚类}
\NormalTok{row\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{5}  \CommentTok{\# 行聚类的数量}
\NormalTok{row\_km }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(data\_large, }\AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ row\_k)}

\CommentTok{\# 对列（样本）进行K{-}means聚类}
\NormalTok{col\_k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{4}  \CommentTok{\# 列聚类的数量}
\NormalTok{col\_km }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{t}\NormalTok{(data\_large), }\AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ col\_k)}

\CommentTok{\# 根据K{-}means聚类结果创建行和列注释}
\NormalTok{row\_ha }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rowAnnotation}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{cluster =} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(row\_km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster))}
\NormalTok{col\_ha }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{HeatmapAnnotation}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{cluster =} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(col\_km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{ux6ce8ux91caux5185ux5bb9}{%
\subsection{注释内容}\label{ux6ce8ux91caux5185ux5bb9}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# 创建行和列注释内容}
\NormalTok{gene\_annotation }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{Gene =} \FunctionTok{rownames}\NormalTok{(data\_large),}
  \AttributeTok{Description =} \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"描述"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{50}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{sample\_annotation }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{Sample =} \FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(data\_large),}
  \AttributeTok{Type =} \FunctionTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Type1"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Type2"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Type3"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Type4"}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{each =} \DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# 添加行和列注释}
\NormalTok{row\_ha }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rowAnnotation}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{cluster =} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(row\_km}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster),}
  \AttributeTok{Gene =} \FunctionTok{anno\_text}\NormalTok{(gene\_annotation}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Description)}
\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
